<a name="client"></a> 
### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ac88-929">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-929">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-930">No [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], o Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) contém modificações e aperfeiçoamentos nas seguintes áreas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-930">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) contains changes and improvements in the following areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-931">O novo controle <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon>, que permite que você implemente uma interface de usuário da faixa de opções que hospeda uma Barra de Ferramentas de Acesso Rápido, um menu do aplicativo e guias.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-931">The new <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> control, which enables you to implement a ribbon user interface that hosts a Quick Access Toolbar, Application Menu, and tabs.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-932">A nova interface <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo>, que dá suporte à validação de dados síncronos e assíncronos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-932">The new <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> interface, which supports synchronous and asynchronous data validation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-933">Novos recursos para as classes <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> e <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-933">New features for the <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> and <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-934">Desempenho melhorado durante a exibição de grandes conjuntos de dados agrupados e o acesso a coleções em threads que não sejam de IU.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-934">Improved performance when displaying large sets of grouped data, and by accessing collections on non-UI threads.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-935">Associação de dados a propriedades estáticas, associação de dados a tipos personalizados que implementam a interface <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> e a recuperação de informações de associação de dados de uma expressão de associação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-935">Data binding to static properties, data binding to custom types that implement the <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> interface, and retrieval of data binding information from a binding expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-936">Reposicionamento de dados à medida que os valores mudam (shaping dinâmico).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-936">Repositioning of data as the values change (live shaping).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-937">Capacidade de verificar se o contexto de dados de um contêiner de itens está desconectado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-937">Ability to check whether the data context for an item container is disconnected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-938">Capacidade de definir o tempo que deve decorrer entre as alterações de propriedade e as atualizações da fonte de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-938">Ability to set the amount of time that should elapse between property changes and data source updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-939">Suporte melhorado para implementar padrões de evento fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-939">Improved support for implementing weak event patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-940">Além disso, os eventos agora podem aceitar extensões de marcação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-940">Also, events can now accept markup extensions.</span></span>

<a name="windows_communication_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-communication-foundation-wcf"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ac88-941">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-941">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-942">No [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], os seguintes recursos foram adicionados para simplificar a gravação e a manutenção de aplicativos do Windows Communication Foundation (WCF):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-942">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the following features have been added to make it simpler to write and maintain Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) applications:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-943">Simplificação de arquivos de configuração gerados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-943">Simplification of generated configuration files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-944">Suporte para desenvolvimento de primeiro contrato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-944">Support for contract-first development.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-945">Capacidade de configurar o modo de compatibilidade do ASP.NET mais facilmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-945">Ability to configure ASP.NET compatibility mode more easily.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-946">Alterações em valores de propriedade de transporte padrão para reduzir a probabilidade de você defini-los.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-946">Changes in default transport property values to reduce the likelihood that you will have to set them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-947">Atualizações feitas na classe <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> reduzem a probabilidade de você precisar configurar manualmente as cotas para leitores de dicionário XML.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-947">Updates to the <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> class to reduce the likelihood that you will have to manually configure quotas for XML dictionary readers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-948">Validação de arquivos de configuração WCF pelo Visual Studio como parte do processo de compilação, de forma que você possa detectar erros de configuração antes de executar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-948">Validation of WCF configuration files by Visual Studio as part of the build process, so you can detect configuration errors before you run your application.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-949">Novo suporte de streaming assíncrono.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-949">New asynchronous streaming support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-950">Novo mapeamento de protocolo HTTPS para facilitar a exposição de um ponto de extremidade em HTTPS com o IIS (Serviços de Informações da Internet).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-950">New HTTPS protocol mapping to make it easier to expose an endpoint over HTTPS with Internet Information Services (IIS).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-951">Capacidade de gerar metadados em um único documento WSDL acrescentando `?singleWSDL` à URL de serviço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-951">Ability to generate metadata in a single WSDL document by appending `?singleWSDL` to the service URL.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-952">Suporte de Websockets para habilitar comunicação bidirecional real em portas 80 e 443 com as características de desempenho semelhantes ao transporte TCP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-952">Websockets support to enable true bidirectional communication over ports 80 and 443 with performance characteristics similar to the TCP transport.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-953">Suporte para configurar serviços no código.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-953">Support for configuring services in code.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-954">Dicas de ferramenta do Editor de XML</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-954">XML Editor tooltips.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-955">Suporte ao armazenamento em cache <xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-955"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> caching support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-956">Suporte à compactação de codificador binário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-956">Binary encoder compression support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-957">Suporte para um transporte UDP que permite que os desenvolvedores gravem serviços que usem o sistema de mensagens "acionar e esquecer".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-957">Support for a UDP transport that enables developers to write services that use "fire and forget" messaging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-958">Um cliente envia uma mensagem para um serviço e não espera nenhuma resposta do serviço.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-958">A client sends a message to a service and expects no response from the service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-959">Capacidade de dar suporte a vários modos de autenticação em um único ponto de extremidade WCF durante o uso do transporte HTTP e da segurança de transporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-959">Ability to support multiple authentication modes on a single WCF endpoint when using the HTTP transport and transport security.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-960">Suporte para serviços WCF que usam IDNs (nomes de domínio internacionalizados).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-960">Support for WCF services that use internationalized domain names (IDNs).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-961">Para saber mais, confira [Novidades no Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-961">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span></span>

<a name="windows_workflow_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-workflow-foundation-wf"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ac88-962">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-962">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-963">No [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], vários recursos novos foram adicionados ao Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), incluindo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-963">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], several new features were added to Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), including:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-964">Os fluxos de trabalho do computador de estado, que foram introduzidos pela primeira vez como parte do .Net Framework 4.0.1 ([Atualização 1 da Plataforma .NET Framework 4](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-964">State machine workflows, which were first introduced as part of the .NET Framework 4.0.1 ([.NET Framework 4 Platform Update 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-965">Essa atualização incluiu várias classes e atividades novas que permitiram que os desenvolvedores criassem fluxos de trabalho de computador do estado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-965">This update included several new classes and activities that enabled developers to create state machine workflows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-966">Essas classes e atividades foram atualizadas para que o [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] inclua:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-966">These classes and activities were updated for the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] to include:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-967">A capacidade de definir pontos de interrupção em estados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-967">The ability to set breakpoints on states.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-968">A capacidade de copiar e colar transições no designer de fluxo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-968">The ability to copy and paste transitions in the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-969">Suporte de designer para criação de transição do disparador compartilhado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-969">Designer support for shared trigger transition creation.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-970">Atividades para criar fluxos de trabalho de computador de estado, incluindo: <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State> e <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-970">Activities for creating state machine workflows, including: <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State>, and <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-971">Recursos do Designer de Fluxo de Trabalho aperfeiçoados, como o seguinte:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-971">Enhanced Workflow Designer features such as the following:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-972">Capacidades de pesquisa do fluxo de trabalho aperfeiçoado no Visual Studio, incluindo **Localização Rápida** e **Localizar nos Arquivos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-972">Enhanced workflow search capabilities in Visual Studio, including **Quick Find** and **Find in Files**.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-973">Capacidade de criar automaticamente uma atividade de Sequência quando uma segunda atividade filho é adicionada a uma atividade de contêiner e de incluir ambas as atividades na atividade de Sequência.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-973">Ability to automatically create a Sequence activity when a second child activity is added to a container activity, and to include both activities in the Sequence activity.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-974">Suporte a movimento panorâmico, o que permite que a parte visível de um fluxo de trabalho seja alterada sem o uso das barras de rolagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-974">Panning support, which enables the visible portion of a workflow to be changed without using the scroll bars.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-975">Uma nova exibição **Estrutura de Tópicos de Documentos** mostra os componentes de um fluxo de trabalho em uma exibição de contorno em estilo árvore e permite selecionar um componente na exibição **Estrutura de Tópicos de Documentos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-975">A new **Document Outline** view that shows the components of a workflow in a tree-style outline view and lets you select a component in the **Document Outline** view.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-976">Capacidade de adicionar anotações a atividades.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-976">Ability to add annotations to activities.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-977">Capacidade de definir e consumir representantes de atividade usando-se o designer de fluxo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-977">Ability to define and consume activity delegates by using the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-978">Conexão e inserção automática para atividades e transições na máquina de estado e fluxos de trabalho do fluxograma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-978">Auto-connect and auto-insert for activities and transitions in state machine and flowchart workflows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-979">Armazenamento das informações do estado de exibição para um fluxo de trabalho em um único elemento no arquivo XAML, logo, você pode localizar e editar facilmente as informações de estado de exibição.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-979">Storage of the view state information for a workflow in a single element in the XAML file, so you can easily locate and edit the view state information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-980">Uma atividade de contêiner NoPersistScope para impedir que as atividades filho persistam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-980">A NoPersistScope container activity to prevent child activities from persisting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-981">Suporte para expressões do C#:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-981">Support for C# expressions:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-982">Os projetos de fluxo de trabalho que usam o Visual Basic usarão expressões do Visual Basic e os projetos de fluxo de trabalho do C# usarão as expressões do C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-982">Workflow projects that use Visual Basic will use Visual Basic expressions, and C# workflow projects will use C# expressions.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-983">Projetos de fluxo de trabalho do C# criados no Visual Studio 2010 e com expressões do Visual Basic são compatíveis com projetos do fluxo de trabalho do C# que usem expressões do C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-983">C# workflow projects that were created in Visual Studio 2010 and that have Visual Basic expressions are compatible with C# workflow projects that use C# expressions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-984">Aperfeiçoamentos do controle de versão:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-984">Versioning enhancements:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-985">A nova classe <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity>, que fornece um mapeamento entre uma instância mantida de fluxo de trabalho e sua definição de fluxo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-985">The new  <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> class, which provides a mapping between a persisted workflow instance and its workflow definition.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-986">Execução lado a lado de várias versões de fluxo de trabalho no mesmo host, incluindo <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-986">Side-by-side execution of multiple workflow versions in the same host, including <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-987">Na Atualização Dinâmica, a capacidade de modificar a definição de uma instância do fluxo de trabalho persistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-987">In Dynamic Update, the ability to modify the definition of a persisted workflow instance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-988">Implantação do serviço de fluxo de trabalho de primeiro contrato, que fornece suporte para gerar automaticamente atividades para corresponder um contrato de serviço existente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-988">Contract-first workflow service development, which provides support for automatically generating activities to match an existing service contract.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-989">Para saber mais, confira [Novidades no Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-989">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span></span>

<a name="tailored"></a> 
### [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]
 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-990">Os aplicativos [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] foram projetados para fatores forma específicos e aproveitam a capacidade do sistema operacional Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-990">[!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps are designed for specific form factors and leverage the power of the Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-991">Um subconjunto do [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ou 4.5.1 está disponível para compilar aplicativos [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] para o Windows usando o C# ou o Visual Basic.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-991">A subset of the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] or 4.5.1 is available for building [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps for Windows by using C# or Visual Basic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-992">Esse subconjunto é chamado de [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] e abordado em uma [visão geral](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) no Windows Dev Center.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-992">This subset is called [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] and is discussed in an [overview](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) in the Windows Dev Center.</span></span>

<a name="portable"></a> 
### <a name="portable-class-libraries"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ac88-993">Bibliotecas de Classes Portáteis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-993">Portable Class Libraries</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-994">O projeto Biblioteca de Classes Portátil no [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (e em versões posteriores) permite gravar e compilar assemblies gerenciados que funcionem em várias plataformas do .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-994">The Portable Class Library project in [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (and later versions) enables you to write and build managed assemblies that work on multiple .NET Framework platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-995">Ao usar um projeto Biblioteca de Classes Portátil, você escolhe as plataformas (como o Windows Phone e o [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]) para direcionar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-995">Using a Portable Class Library project, you choose the platforms (such as Windows Phone and [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]) to target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-996">Os tipos e membros disponíveis em seu projeto são restritos automaticamente aos tipos e membros comuns através dessas plataformas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-996">The available types and members in your project are automatically restricted to the common types and members across these platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ac88-997">Para saber mais, confira [Biblioteca de Classes Portátil](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ac88-997">For more information, see [Portable Class Library](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span></span>
